#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Created on Wed Jan  3 14:49:32 2018

@author: malekzadeh
"""
###############################################################################
import sys
sys.path.append('./moh_lib')
import cnn_act_rec_v5 as cnn_act_rec
import ts2secs
import dataset_builder_v2 as dsbldr
import numpy as np
###############################################################################

vld_vrb = 1
evl_vrb = 0
num_folds = 4

dsinfs = dsbldr.get_ds_infos()
print("\nData Subjects Info is Created: shape = ",dsinfs.shape)
subjects = dsinfs[:,0]
activity_list = {'dwn':1, 'up':2, 'sit':3, 'std':4, 'wlk':5, 'jog':6}
activity = activity_list['wlk']
attribute_list = {'weight':1, 'height':2, 'age':3, 'gender':4}
attribute = attribute_list['height']

if attribute != 4: 
    typeof = "reg" ## regression
    avg_mae = 0
    avg_rmse = 0
else:
    typeof = "cla" ## classification
    losses = np.zeros(num_folds)
    accuracies = np.zeros(num_folds)
    cf_rprt = {}
    cf_cfmt = {}

for fold in range(1,num_folds+1):
    print("\n---->> ## Fold ",fold,":")
    train_list = []
    validate_list = []
    test_list = []
    
    """
    -> 75% of the subjects for on training the model and 
    -> 25% are used for testing the learned model.
    """    
    for j in range(len(subjects)):
        if j%num_folds == fold-1 and len(test_list) < (len(subjects)//4):
            test_list.append(int(subjects[j]))
            continue
        train_list.append(int(subjects[j]))    
    print("Test List is = ",test_list)

    """
    -> 20% of the subjects in training list  are used for 
    validation in training phase.
    """
    for i in range(len(train_list)//5):
        validate_list.append(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
        train_list.remove(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
    print("Train List is = ",train_list)
    print("Validate List is = ",validate_list)

    
    
    print("\nCreat Dataset for '",activity,"' Activity:")
    train_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, train_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Training dataset: shape = ",train_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    validate_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, validate_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Validation dataset: shape = ",validate_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    test_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, test_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Test dataset: shape = ",test_one_by_gender.shape)
        
                    
    ## Train Model on Similar
    print("_____________________________________________")
    print("Learning: Weight Regression")
    train_data, train_labels , mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(train_one_by_gender,
                                                                         standardize = True)

    validate_data, validate_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(validate_one_by_gender,
                                                                               standardize = True,
                                                                               mean = mean, std = std)
    
    test_data, test_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(test_one_by_gender,
                                                                       standardize = True,
                                                                       mean = mean, std = std)
    
    typeof= "reg"
    maeh = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=100,
                      vbs=2,
                      validate= True
                      )
    maeh = np.array(maeh)
    maeh[:4] = max(maeh)
    epoc = (np.array(maeh)).argmin() + 1
    
    rmse, mae = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=epoc,
                      vbs=0,
                      validate= False
                      )
    
    avg_rmse = avg_rmse+rmse
    avg_mae = avg_mae+mae    
    
print("********* Fianl Root Mean Squared Error:", str(round(avg_rmse/num_folds,2)) )    
print("********* Fianl Mean Absolute Error:", str(round(avg_mae/num_folds,2) ))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Created on Wed Jan  3 14:49:32 2018

@author: malekzadeh
"""
###############################################################################
import sys
sys.path.append('./moh_lib')
import cnn_act_rec_v5 as cnn_act_rec
import ts2secs
import dataset_builder_v2 as dsbldr
import numpy as np
###############################################################################

vld_vrb = 1
evl_vrb = 0
num_folds = 4

dsinfs = dsbldr.get_ds_infos()
print("\nData Subjects Info is Created: shape = ",dsinfs.shape)
subjects = dsinfs[:,0]
activity_list = {'dwn':1, 'up':2, 'sit':3, 'std':4, 'wlk':5, 'jog':6}
activity = activity_list['wlk']
attribute_list = {'weight':1, 'height':2, 'age':3, 'gender':4, 'bmi':5}
attribute = attribute_list['bmi']

if attribute != 4: 
    typeof = "reg" ## regression
    avg_mae = 0
    avg_rmse = 0
else:
    typeof = "cla" ## classification
    losses = np.zeros(num_folds)
    accuracies = np.zeros(num_folds)
    cf_rprt = {}
    cf_cfmt = {}

for fold in range(1,num_folds+1):
    print("\n---->> ## Fold ",fold,":")
    train_list = []
    validate_list = []
    test_list = []
    
    """
    -> 75% of the subjects for on training the model and 
    -> 25% are used for testing the learned model.
    """    
    for j in range(len(subjects)):
        if j%num_folds == fold-1 and len(test_list) < (len(subjects)//4):
            test_list.append(int(subjects[j]))
            continue
        train_list.append(int(subjects[j]))    
    print("Test List is = ",test_list)

    """
    -> 20% of the subjects in training list  are used for 
    validation in training phase.
    """
    for i in range(len(train_list)//5):
        validate_list.append(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
        train_list.remove(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
    print("Train List is = ",train_list)
    print("Validate List is = ",validate_list)

    
    
    print("\nCreat Dataset for '",activity,"' Activity:")
    train_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, train_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Training dataset: shape = ",train_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    validate_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, validate_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Validation dataset: shape = ",validate_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    test_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, test_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Test dataset: shape = ",test_one_by_gender.shape)
        
                    
    ## Train Model on Similar
    print("_____________________________________________")
    print("Learning: Weight Regression")
    train_data, train_labels , mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(train_one_by_gender,
                                                                         standardize = True)

    validate_data, validate_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(validate_one_by_gender,
                                                                               standardize = True,
                                                                               mean = mean, std = std)
    
    test_data, test_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(test_one_by_gender,
                                                                       standardize = True,
                                                                       mean = mean, std = std)
    
    typeof= "reg"
    maeh = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=100,
                      vbs=2,
                      validate= True
                      )
    maeh = np.array(maeh)
    maeh[:4] = max(maeh)
    epoc = (np.array(maeh)).argmin() + 1
    
    rmse, mae = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=epoc,
                      vbs=0,
                      validate= False
                      )
    
    avg_rmse = avg_rmse+rmse
    avg_mae = avg_mae+mae    
    
print("********* Fianl Root Mean Squared Error:", str(round(avg_rmse/num_folds,2)) )    
print("********* Fianl Mean Absolute Error:", str(round(avg_mae/num_folds,2) ))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Created on Wed Jan  3 14:49:32 2018

@author: malekzadeh
"""
###############################################################################
import sys
sys.path.append('./moh_lib')
import cnn_act_rec_v5 as cnn_act_rec
import ts2secs
import dataset_builder_v2 as dsbldr
import numpy as np
###############################################################################

vld_vrb = 1
evl_vrb = 0
num_folds = 4

dsinfs = dsbldr.get_ds_infos()
print("\nData Subjects Info is Created: shape = ",dsinfs.shape)
subjects = dsinfs[:,0]
activity_list = {'dwn':1, 'up':2, 'sit':3, 'std':4, 'wlk':5, 'jog':6}
activity = activity_list['wlk']
attribute_list = {'weight':1, 'height':2, 'age':3, 'gender':4, 'bmi':5}
attribute = attribute_list['age']

if attribute != 4: 
    typeof = "reg" ## regression
    avg_mae = 0
    avg_rmse = 0
else:
    typeof = "cla" ## classification
    losses = np.zeros(num_folds)
    accuracies = np.zeros(num_folds)
    cf_rprt = {}
    cf_cfmt = {}

for fold in range(1,num_folds+1):
    print("\n---->> ## Fold ",fold,":")
    train_list = []
    validate_list = []
    test_list = []
    
    """
    -> 75% of the subjects for on training the model and 
    -> 25% are used for testing the learned model.
    """    
    for j in range(len(subjects)):
        if j%num_folds == fold-1 and len(test_list) < (len(subjects)//4):
            test_list.append(int(subjects[j]))
            continue
        train_list.append(int(subjects[j]))    
    print("Test List is = ",test_list)

    """
    -> 20% of the subjects in training list  are used for 
    validation in training phase.
    """
    for i in range(len(train_list)//5):
        validate_list.append(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
        train_list.remove(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
    print("Train List is = ",train_list)
    print("Validate List is = ",validate_list)

    
    
    print("\nCreat Dataset for '",activity,"' Activity:")
    train_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, train_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Training dataset: shape = ",train_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    validate_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, validate_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Validation dataset: shape = ",validate_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    test_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, test_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Test dataset: shape = ",test_one_by_gender.shape)
        
                    
    ## Train Model on Similar
    print("_____________________________________________")
    print("Learning: Weight Regression")
    train_data, train_labels , mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(train_one_by_gender,
                                                                         standardize = True)

    validate_data, validate_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(validate_one_by_gender,
                                                                               standardize = True,
                                                                               mean = mean, std = std)
    
    test_data, test_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(test_one_by_gender,
                                                                       standardize = True,
                                                                       mean = mean, std = std)
    
    typeof= "reg"
    maeh = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=100,
                      vbs=2,
                      validate= True
                      )
    maeh = np.array(maeh)
    maeh[:4] = max(maeh)
    epoc = (np.array(maeh)).argmin() + 1
    
    rmse, mae = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=epoc,
                      vbs=0,
                      validate= False
                      )
    
    avg_rmse = avg_rmse+rmse
    avg_mae = avg_mae+mae    
    
print("********* Fianl Root Mean Squared Error:", str(round(avg_rmse/num_folds,2)) )    
print("********* Fianl Mean Absolute Error:", str(round(avg_mae/num_folds,2) ))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
Created on Wed Jan  3 14:49:32 2018

@author: malekzadeh
"""
###############################################################################
import sys
sys.path.append('./moh_lib')
import cnn_act_rec_v5 as cnn_act_rec
import ts2secs
import dataset_builder_v2 as dsbldr
import numpy as np
###############################################################################

vld_vrb = 1
evl_vrb = 0
num_folds = 4

dsinfs = dsbldr.get_ds_infos()
print("\nData Subjects Info is Created: shape = ",dsinfs.shape)
subjects = dsinfs[:,0]
activity_list = {'dwn':1, 'up':2, 'sit':3, 'std':4, 'wlk':5, 'jog':6}
activity = activity_list['wlk']
attribute_list = {'weight':1, 'height':2, 'age':3, 'gender':4, 'bmi':5}
attribute = attribute_list['weight']

if attribute != 4: 
    typeof = "reg" ## regression
    avg_mae = 0
    avg_rmse = 0
else:
    typeof = "cla" ## classification
    losses = np.zeros(num_folds)
    accuracies = np.zeros(num_folds)
    cf_rprt = {}
    cf_cfmt = {}

for fold in range(1,num_folds+1):
    print("\n---->> ## Fold ",fold,":")
    train_list = []
    validate_list = []
    test_list = []
    
    """
    -> 75% of the subjects for on training the model and 
    -> 25% are used for testing the learned model.
    """    
    for j in range(len(subjects)):
        if j%num_folds == fold-1 and len(test_list) < (len(subjects)//4):
            test_list.append(int(subjects[j]))
            continue
        train_list.append(int(subjects[j]))    
    print("Test List is = ",test_list)

    """
    -> 20% of the subjects in training list  are used for 
    validation in training phase.
    """
    for i in range(len(train_list)//5):
        validate_list.append(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
        train_list.remove(train_list[fold+i*5-1])
    print("Train List is = ",train_list)
    print("Validate List is = ",validate_list)

    
    
    print("\nCreat Dataset for '",activity,"' Activity:")
    train_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, train_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Training dataset: shape = ",train_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    validate_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, validate_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Validation dataset: shape = ",validate_one_by_gender.shape)
    
    test_one_by_gender = dsbldr.merge(dsinfs, activity, attribute, test_list)
    print("shape of '",activity,"' acitviy Test dataset: shape = ",test_one_by_gender.shape)
        
                    
    ## Train Model on Similar
    print("_____________________________________________")
    print("Learning: Weight Regression")
    train_data, train_labels , mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(train_one_by_gender,
                                                                         standardize = True)

    validate_data, validate_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(validate_one_by_gender,
                                                                               standardize = True,
                                                                               mean = mean, std = std)
    
    test_data, test_labels, mean, std = ts2secs.time_series_to_section(test_one_by_gender,
                                                                       standardize = True,
                                                                       mean = mean, std = std)
    
    typeof= "reg"
    maeh = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=100,
                      vbs=2,
                      validate= True
                      )
    maeh = np.array(maeh)
    maeh[:4] = max(maeh)
    epoc = (np.array(maeh)).argmin() + 1
    
    rmse, mae = cnn_act_rec.train(typeof,
                      train_data,
                      train_labels,
                      test_data,
                      test_labels,
                      validate_data,
                      validate_labels,
                      epoc=epoc,
                      vbs=0,
                      validate= False
                      )
    
    avg_rmse = avg_rmse+rmse
    avg_mae = avg_mae+mae    
    
print("********* Final Root Mean Squared Error:", str(round(avg_rmse/num_folds,2)) )    
print("********* Final Mean Absolute Error:", str(round(avg_mae/num_folds,2) ))
